\subsection*{Additional Inherited Members}


\subsection{Detailed Description}
This class extends \hyperlink{classns3_1_1Asn1Header}{Asn1\+Header} functions, adding serialization/deserialization of some Information elements defined in 3\+G\+PP TS 36.\+331

\subsection{Member Function Documentation}
\index{ns3\+::\+Rrc\+Asn1\+Header@{ns3\+::\+Rrc\+Asn1\+Header}!Deserialize@{Deserialize}}
\index{Deserialize@{Deserialize}!ns3\+::\+Rrc\+Asn1\+Header@{ns3\+::\+Rrc\+Asn1\+Header}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{Deserialize(\+Buffer\+::\+Iterator b\+Iterator)=0}{Deserialize(Buffer::Iterator bIterator)=0}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}uint32\+\_\+t ns3\+::\+Rrc\+Asn1\+Header\+::\+Deserialize (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf Buffer\+::\+Iterator}}]{start}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}\hypertarget{classns3_1_1RrcAsn1Header_afbb8ee5709d02eca06349cd26052108a}{}\label{classns3_1_1RrcAsn1Header_afbb8ee5709d02eca06349cd26052108a}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em start} & an iterator which points to where the header should read from. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the number of bytes read.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This method is used by \hyperlink{classns3_1_1Packet_a0961eccf975d75f902d40956c93ba63e}{Packet\+::\+Remove\+Header} to re-\/create a header from the byte buffer of a packet. The data read is expected to match bit-\/for-\/bit the representation of this header in real networks.

Note that data is not actually removed from the buffer to which the iterator points. Both \hyperlink{classns3_1_1Packet_a0961eccf975d75f902d40956c93ba63e}{Packet\+::\+Remove\+Header()} and \hyperlink{classns3_1_1Packet_aadc63487bea70945c418f4c3e9b81964}{Packet\+::\+Peek\+Header()} call \hyperlink{classns3_1_1RrcAsn1Header_afbb8ee5709d02eca06349cd26052108a}{Deserialize()}, but only the Remove\+Header() has additional statements to remove the header bytes from the underlying buffer and associated metadata. 

Implements \hyperlink{classns3_1_1Asn1Header_a4664472c9288585a19f4f92202f490c0}{ns3\+::\+Asn1\+Header}.

\index{ns3\+::\+Rrc\+Asn1\+Header@{ns3\+::\+Rrc\+Asn1\+Header}!Pre\+Serialize@{Pre\+Serialize}}
\index{Pre\+Serialize@{Pre\+Serialize}!ns3\+::\+Rrc\+Asn1\+Header@{ns3\+::\+Rrc\+Asn1\+Header}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{Pre\+Serialize(void) const =0}{PreSerialize(void) const =0}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}virtual void ns3\+::\+Rrc\+Asn1\+Header\+::\+Pre\+Serialize (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{void}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}\hypertarget{classns3_1_1RrcAsn1Header_a4ae9d9c61fb27223e3ed4360d4344893}{}\label{classns3_1_1RrcAsn1Header_a4ae9d9c61fb27223e3ed4360d4344893}
This function serializes class attributes to m\+\_\+serialization\+Result local \hyperlink{classns3_1_1Buffer}{Buffer}. As A\+S\+N1 encoding produces a bitstream that does not have a fixed length, this function is needed to store the result, so its length can be retrieved with \hyperlink{classns3_1_1Header_a6ef0497eabc1b1fb0ad42738eb73f934}{Header\+::\+Get\+Serialized\+Size()} function. This method is pure virtual in this class (needs to be implemented in child classes) as the meaningful information elements are in the subclasses. 

Implements \hyperlink{classns3_1_1Asn1Header_a93ff29103b4090ed77666e3ac3aeae19}{ns3\+::\+Asn1\+Header}.

\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{Print(std\+::ostream \&os) const }{Print(std::ostream &os) const }}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void ns3\+::\+Rrc\+Asn1\+Header\+::\+Print (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{std\+::ostream \&}]{os}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}\hypertarget{classns3_1_1RrcAsn1Header_ac928fb6bdda0c08fe091355774582d55}{}\label{classns3_1_1RrcAsn1Header_ac928fb6bdda0c08fe091355774582d55}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em os} & output stream This method is used by \hyperlink{classns3_1_1Packet_aa34058a5cdbf94673531f8c4001ab227}{Packet\+::\+Print} to print the content of a header as ascii data to a c++ output stream. Although the header is free to format its output as it wishes, it is recommended to follow a few rules to integrate with the packet pretty printer\+: start with flags, small field values located between a pair of parens. Values should be separated by whitespace. Follow the parens with the important fields, separated by whitespace. i.\+e.\+: (field1 val1 field2 val2 field3 val3) field4 val4 field5 val5 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}


Implements \hyperlink{classns3_1_1Asn1Header_a8b7c035ddfef790a32477dc8895ea99b}{ns3\+::\+Asn1\+Header}.
